<initial_plan>

1) **Hard Constraints**
- Property must be located in **Toronto**.  
- Budget range is **CAD $420,000–$480,000**.  
- Property type: **1–2 bedroom modern condo**.  
- Must have **creative workspace potential** (e.g., open layout, good lighting, designated office area).  
- Joint purchase between **user and Alex**.  

2) **Soft Constraints**
- Preference for newer or well-renovated buildings.  
- Access to amenities (e.g., gym, co-working lounge) is a plus.  
- Ideally near transit and downtown core or creative districts (e.g., Liberty Village, Distillery District, Leslieville).  
- Reasonable monthly maintenance fees.  

3) **Task Decomposition**
a) **Property Selection**  
   - Contact external real estate agent for available listings matching criteria.  
   - Compare 3–5 most suitable options with price, size, location, and unique workspace potential.  

b) **Financing Solutions**  
   - Explore joint mortgage options within budget.  
   - Identify down payment and estimated monthly mortgage payments.  
   - Review terms (interest rate, amortization, pre-approval possibilities).  

c) **Legal and Survey Arrangements**  
   - Find real estate lawyer(s) specializing in condo purchases in Toronto.  
   - Request estimated fees for legal review, title search, and closing costs.  
   - Include property survey or status certificate review costs.  

d) **Moving Services**  
   - Obtain quotes for moving services within Toronto.  
   - Estimate cost for packing and transport.  

e) **Setup and Utilities**  
   - Roughly coordinate setup services (hydro, internet, condo management setup).  
   - Estimate monthly utility and maintenance costs.  

f) **Total Budget Summary**  
   - Combine property cost + financing + legal + moving + setup into a complete cost breakdown.  

4) **Data Planning (Environment Requests)**
- Request user’s full name (for joint financing and purchase documents).  
- Request Alex’s full name (for joint ownership context).  
- Gather user’s current employment and income details if needed for financing pre-approval.  
- Retrieve any previous mortgage or property purchase history (if available).  

5) **Anticipated Changes**
- Property selection may shift slightly if listings under CAD $480K are limited.  
- Financing terms may vary depending on lender’s pre-approval criteria.  
- Legal and moving service costs may adjust depending on specific condo location and closing timeline.  

</initial_plan>
